<s> act i the scene is the pretty drawing room of a flat <\s>
<s> there are two doors one open into the hall the other shut and curtained <\s>
<s> through a large bay window the curtains of which are not yet drawn the towers of westminster can be seen darkening in a summer sunset a grand piano stands across one corner <\s>
<s> the man servant paynter clean shaven and discreet is arranging two tables for bridge <\s>
<s> burney the maid a girl with one of those flowery botticellian faces only met with in england comes in through the curtained door which she leaves open disclosing the glimpse of a white wall <\s>
<s> paynter looks up at her she shakes her head with an expression of concern <\s>
<s> just walks about i fancy <\s>
